10a1(khri brgyad): nas tshangs ris dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed dang / 'phrul dga' dang / dga' ldan dang / 'tha' thal dang / sbrum cu rtsa gsam
10a2(khri brgyad): ba dang / rgyal chen bzhi'i lha'i ris kyi bar ji snyed yod pa de dag thams cad kyis de bzhin gshegs rnap+la skye ba'i mchog mi shes pa mthong nas/ de dag tshim zhing
10a3(khri brgyad): mgu la yid rangs ste/ rab tu dga' nas dga'ang yid bde ba skyes ste/ lha'i me tog dag khyer zhing lha'i me tog 'phreng ba dang / lha'i spos dang / lha'i
10a4(khri brgyad): byug pa dang / lha'i phye ma dang / la'i gdug pa dang / lha'i ud pal dang / pad+ma dang / ku mu daM dang / pad+ma dkar po dang / na lin dang / dri mchog dang / lha'i me
10a5(khri brgyad): tog klu shing me tog dang / ta ma la' mye tog dang / lha'i gos dang / lha'i rgyan dang / lha'i gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / bangag khyer te/ bcom
10a6(khri brgyad): ldan 'das ga la ba der dong ngo // stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'di ni 'dul ba dang snod du gyur pa'i ming gang dag 'khod pa de dag gis kyang
10a7(khri brgyad): de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku lta bas mchog mi shes pa mthong nas/ zang las skyes pa dang / chu las skyes pa'i me tog rnams khyer te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i
10a8(khri brgyad): srubasapas mchog ma shes pa gal ba der dong ngo // de nas / de dag drang / mau de dag gis lha'i me tog dang / spos dang / bdug pa dang / me tog dang / zeng sa
10b1(khri brgyad): ba dang / byug pa dang / phye ma dang / gos dang / gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan de dag dang / chu las skyes pa dang / zang las skyes pa'i me tog de
10b2(khri brgyad): ngag de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku la gtor mngon par gtor mngon par rab tu gtor to// de nas me tog dang / spos dang / me tog dang phreng ba dang / byug pa dang
10b3(khri brgyad): phye ma dang / gos dang / gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan gyi char dang / thang las skyes pa dang / chu las skyes pa'i me tog gang dag bcom ldan 'das
10b4(khri brgyad): la gtor ba de dag thams cad bcom ldan 'das kyis byin gyis rlabs kyis bcom ldan 'das kyi dbu'i drang tha~Md kyi steng nam mkha' la khang pa brtsegs pa stong gsuM
10b5(khri brgyad): gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi tshad tsam gcig tu red de gnas par gyur to// khang pa brtsegs pa de las kyang lha'i me tog dang / dar gyi lnga ldi dag
10b6(khri brgyad): phyang rab tu 'phyang / mngon par rab tu 'phyang ste/ me tog gi lda ldi dang / dar gyi lnga ldi de dag gis kyang stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams
10b7(khri brgyad): 'di shin tu mdzes par gyur to// bcom ldan 'das kyi 'od snang ba gser gyi kha dog lta bu phyogs bcur 'phros pa des kyang / phyogs re rer 'jig rten gyi khams
10b8(khri brgyad): gang+gA'i glang gi bye ma snyed ngag khyab par sdang bar gyur to// stong gsum gyi sgong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'dzin 'dzam bu gling gi 'jig rten khams thams cad
11a1(khri brgyad): rnams dang/ ga
11a2(khri brgyad): kyi lha dang mi dgaso so nas 'di snyam du sems te/ de bzhin gshegs pa ni bdag gi mdun na bzhugs shing chos stan to snyam mo// de bzhin
11a3(khri brgyad): nub kyi ba lang spyod dang / shar gyi lus 'phags dang / byang gi sgra mi snyan dang / rgyal chen bzhi'i ris kyi lha rnams kyi bar dang / de bzhin du steng gi 'jig rten gyi
11a4(khri brgyad): dang / stong gnyis kyi 'jig rten gyi khams dang / stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi lha dang / mi de dag thams cad 'di snyam du sems te/
11a5(khri brgyad): bzhin gshegs pa ni bdag cag gi mdun na bzhugs shing chos ston to snyam mo// de nas bcom ldan 'das gdan seng ge'i khri nyid la bzhugs bzhin du yang 'dzum
11a6(khri brgyad): ba mdzad de/ 'dzum pa'i sdang ba des stong gsum gyi chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'di gsal bar gyur te/ stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams
11a7(khri brgyad): 'di na sems can gang dag 'khod pa de dag thams cad kyis shar phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi gang+gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed dag na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das nyan thos kyi
11a8(khri brgyad): dge 'dun dang bcas pa dag mthong bar gyur to// shar phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams gang+gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed dag na/ sems can gang dag 'khod pa de dag gis
11a9(khri brgyad): kyang 'jig rten gyi khams mi mjed 'di dang / bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa dge slong gi dge 'dun dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs pa mthong ngo // de bzhin du 'jig
11b1(khri brgyad): gyi khams mi mjed du gtogs pa'i sems can rnams kyis/ lho dang / nub dang / byang phyogs dang / byang shar dang / shar sgo dang / lho nub dang / nub byang gi phyogs
11b2(khri brgyad): mtshams dang / 'og dang steng gi phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams gang+gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed dag na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das nyan thos kyi dge 'dun dang zab
11b3(khri brgyad): gcig tu bzhugs pa dag mthong ngo // 'jig rten gyi khams gang+gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed dag na/ sems can gang dag 'khod pa de dag gis kyang 'jig rten gyi
11b4(khri brgyad): khams mi mjed 'di dang / bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa dge slong gi dge 'dun dang / thabs gcig tu bzhugs pa mthong ngo // de nas shar phyogs su 'jig
11b5(khri brgyad): rten gyi khams gang+gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed 'das pa kun gyi pha rol na/ 'jig rten gyi khams rin chen zhes bya ba yod de/ de na de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa
11b6(khri brgyad): yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas dkon mchog 'byung gnas shes bya ba da ltar bzhugs te 'tsho zhing gzhes so// de byang chub sems dpa' rnams la shes
11b7(khri brgyad): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'di nyid ston to// de nas 'jig rten gyi khams de na/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun nas 'od gzer zhes bya ba 'dug
11b8(khri brgyad): pas snang ba chen po de dang / sa cher g.yos pa de dang / bcom ldan 'das kyi sku blta ba'i mchog mi shes pa de mthong nas/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gan/
12a1(khri brgyad): pa dkon mchog 'byung gnas gal ba der dong ste byin nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa dkon mchog 'byung gnas de la 'di skad ces gsol
12a2(khri brgyad): to// bcom ldan 'das snang ba chen po 'jig rten du byung ba 'di dang / dogs cher g.yos pa 'di dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku sta bas mchog ma shes pa 'da'
12a3(khri brgyad): 'di'i rgyu gang lags/ rkyen gang lags/ de skad ces gsol ba dang / bcom ldan 'das dkon mchog 'byung gnas kyis byang chub sems dpa' kun nas 'od ga
12a4(khri brgyad): la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rigs kyi bu nub phyogs su 'jig rten gyi khams gang+gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed 'das pa na 'jig rten gyi khams mi mjed ces bya
12a5(khri brgyad): ba yod de/ de na de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa zhes bya ba da ltar bzhugs te 'tsho zhing gnyis la/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams la chos ston te/ 'di ni
12a6(khri brgyad): de'i mthu yin de 'dra'o// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dkon mchog 'byung la/ byang chub sems dpa' kun nas 'od gzer gyis 'di skad ces gsol to//
12a7(khri brgyad): bcom ldan 'das bdag bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thu ba de la blta ba dang / phyag bgyi ba dang / bsnyen bkur bgyi ba dang / byang chub
12a8(khri brgyad): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag kyang bal cher gzhon nur gyur pa/ gzungs dang so so yang dag par rig pa thob pa/ ting nge 'dzin dang snyoms par
12b1(khri brgyad): 'jug pa thams cad la dbang thob pa/ de dag blta ba'i slad du 'jig rten gyi khams mi mjed du 'chi'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal ba/ rigs
12b2(khri brgyad): bu de'i dus la dbab par shes na khyod song shig/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dkon mchog 'byung gnas kyis/ byang chub sems dpa' kun nas 'od gan
12b3(khri brgyad): la pad+ma rin po che sna tshogs kyi rgyu las byung ba gser gyi mdog can 'ad ba ma stong dang ldan pa stong skur te/ rigs kyi bu khyod kyis de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub
12b4(khri brgyad): ba de la pad+mo 'di dag gtor cig/ rigs kyi bu khyod sangs rgyas kyi zhing der shes bzhin du spyod cig/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'jig rten gyi khams mi mjed der skyes pa'i
12b5(khri brgyad): byang chub sems dpa' de dag bsnyen par dka' ba'i phyir ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun nas 'od gzer gyis/ de bzhin gshegs pa dkon mchog 'byung
12b6(khri brgyad): gnas las rin po che'i rgyu las byung ba'i pad+ma gser gyi mdog can 'dab ma stong dang ldan pa de dag blangs te/ byang chub sems dpa' khyim pa dang / rab tu byung
12b7(khri brgyad): ba dang / khye'u dang / bu mo bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag du mas yongs su bskor cing mdun du bdar te/ lhan cig tu sangs rgyas kyi zhing de nas mi snang bar gyur na
12b8(khri brgyad): shar phyogs na sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ji snyed bzhugs te 'tsho zhing gzhes pa de dag nyams cad la me tog dang / bdug pa dang / spos dang / me tog phreng
13a1(khri brgyad): dang / thug pa dang / thes dang / gos dang / gdugs dang / rgyas man rung / dad+ma gA sa bsku snang dud+d+ha/ tham rgyas
13a2(khri brgyad): byas/ mchod par byas nas/ byang chub sems dpa'i rdzu 'phrul chen po dang / byang chub sems dpa'i mthu chen pos 'jig rten gyi khams mi mjed gal ba der sbyin na/
13a3(khri brgyad): bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa ga la ba der song nas phyin pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ phyogs gcig tu 'dug go// phyogs bci
13a4(khri brgyad): tu 'dug nas/ byang chub sems dpa' kun nas 'od gzer gyis/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa de la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan
13a5(khri brgyad): 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dkon mchog 'byung gnas/ bcom ldan 'das la bsnyun gsol te/ gnod pa chung ngam/ nyim nga chung ngam/ bskyod pa yang
13a6(khri brgyad): ngam/ 'tsho ba 'am/ stobs dang ldan nam/ bde ba la reg par gnas sam/ zhes bskrun gsol to// bcom ldan 'das dkon mchog 'byung gnas kyis
13a7(khri brgyad): pad+ma 'di dag kyang bcom ldan 'das la bskur ro// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pas pad+ma de dag bzhes nas/ shar phyogs kyi sangs
13a8(khri brgyad): rgyas bcom ldan 'das gang+gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed po de dag ga la ba de logs su gtor to// pad+ma de dag gis 'jig rten gyi khams de dag khyab par gyur te/ badz+ra
13b1(khri brgyad): de dag la sangs rgyas kyi sku dag bzhugs shing / sangs rgyas kyi zhing de dag na/ 'di lta ste shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang ldan pa 'di nyid kyi chos ston to//
13b2(khri brgyad): sems can gang dag gis chos de thos pa de dag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu nges par gyur to// de nas byang chub sems dpa' khyim na gnas
13b3(khri brgyad): pa dang / rab tu byung ba de dag dang / khye'u dang bu mo de dag gis kyang rang rang gi dge ba'i rtsa ba dag gis bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa la
13b4(khri brgyad): bsti stang du byas/ bla mar byas/ ri mor byas/ mchod par byas te/ phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// de nas lho phyogs su 'jig rten gyi khams gang+gA klung gi
13b5(khri brgyad): bye ma snyed 'das pa kun gyi pha rol na/ 'jig rten gyi khams mya ngan thams cad med pa zhes bya ba yod de/ de na de bzhin gyi glegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag
13b6(khri brgyad): par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas mya ngan med pa'i dpal zhes bya ba 'altar bzhugs te 'tsho zhing gzhes so// de na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po mya ngan
13b7(khri brgyad): med pa zhes bya ba 'dug pas shes bya ba nas/ phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// zhes bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar ro// de bzhin du nub phyogs na 'jig rten gyi kham
13b8(khri brgyad): nye bar zhi ba zhes bya ba yod de/ de na de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rin chen 'od 'phro zhes bya ba de ltar bzhugs te/ 'tshe
14a1(khri brgyad): zhing gzhes so// de na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spyod pa'i blo gros shes bya ba 'jug par shes bya ba nas/ phyogs ga
14a2(khri brgyad): tu 'khod do// zhes bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar ro// byang phyogs na 'jig rten gyi kham rgya rgyu ba zhes bya ba yod de/ de na de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa la
14a3(khri brgyad): dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rgyal ba'i dbang po zhes bya ba de ltar bzhugs te 'tsho zhing gzhes so// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos rgyal ba
14a4(khri brgyad): byin zhes bya ba 'dug pas shes bya ba nas/ phyogs cig tu 'khod do zhes bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar ro// de bzhin du byang shar gyi phyogs 'tshams na 'jig rten gyi
14a5(khri brgyad): khams ting nge 'dzin gyis brgyan pa zhes bya ba yod de/ de na de bzhin gshegasu pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangasating nge 'dzin gyi glang po che ngas
14a6(khri brgyad): pa'i dpal zhes bya ba da ltar bzhugs te 'tsho zhing gzhes so// de na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnam par ga non pas rnam par gnon pa zhes bya ba
14a7(khri brgyad): 'dug pas shes bya ba nas phyogs gcig tu 'khod do zhes bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar ro// shar lho'i phyogs mtshams na 'jig rten gyi khams byang chub kyi
14a8(khri brgyad): snying po'i rgyan shin tu mdzes pa zhes bya ba yod de/ de na de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas pad+ma mchog gi dpal zhes bya
14b1(khri brgyad): ba yod de/ de na de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas pad+ma mchog gi dpal zhes bya ba da ltar bzhugs te 'tsho zhing gzheso//
14b2(khri brgyad): de na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po lag na pad+ma zhes bya ba 'dug pas shes bya ba nas phyogs gcig tu 'khod de zhes bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar
14b3(khri brgyad): ro// lho nub kyi phyogs mtshams na 'jig rten gyi khams rdul tshogs dang bral zhes bya ba yod de de na de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs
14b4(khri brgyad): pa'i sangs rgyas nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor sgron ma mchog gi dpal zhes bya ba de ltar bzhugs te 'tsho zhing gzhes so// de na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen
14b5(khri brgyad): po nyi ma'i 'od ces bya ba 'dug pas shes bya ba nas/ phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// zhes bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar ro// nub byang gi phyogs mtshams
14b6(khri brgyad): na 'jig rten gyi khams dbang du gyur pa zhes bya ba yod de don de bzhin gshegs pa dag bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas gdugs gcig pa zhes bya
14b7(khri brgyad): ba da ltar bzhugs te 'tsho zhing gzhes so// de na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rin chen mchog ces bya ba nas phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// zhes
14b8(khri brgyad): bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar ro// 'og gi phyogs na 'jig rten gyi khams pad+ma zhes bya ba yod de/ de na de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs
15a1(khri brgyad): ba'i sangs rgyas pad+ma'i dpal zhes bya ba da ltar bzhugs te 'tsho zhing gzhes so// de na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen
15a2(khri brgyad): po pad+ma mchog ces bya ba 'dug pa shes bya ba nas phyogs gcig tu 'khod do zhes bya ba'i bar du rgyas par sbyar ro// de nas steng gi phyogs su 'jig rten gyi khams
15a3(khri brgyad): gang+gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed 'das pa kun gyi pha rol na 'jig rten gyi khams dga' ba zhes bya ba yod de/ de na de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs
15a4(khri brgyad): pa'i sangs rgyas dga' ba'i dpal zhes bya ba da ltar bzhugs te 'tsho zhing gzhes so// de na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dga' bas byin zhes
15a5(khri brgyad): bya ba 'dug pas snang ba chen po de dang / sa cher g.yos pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku blta bas mchog mi shes pa de mthong nas/ bcom ldan 'das
15a6(khri brgyad): de bzhin gshegs pa dga' ba'i dpal ga la ba der song ste byin nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa dga' ba'i dpal la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan
15a7(khri brgyad): 'das snang ba chen po 'jig rten du byung ba dang / ngogs cher gams pa 'di dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sru bsta bas mchog mi shes pa 'da' ba 'di'i rgyu
15a8(khri brgyad): gang lags rkyen gang lags/ de skad ces gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das dga' ba'i dpal gyis/ byang chub sems dpa' dga' bas byin la 'di
15b1(khri brgyad): skad ces bka' stsal to// rigs kyi 'og gi phyogs su 'jig rten gyi khams gang+gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed 'das pa na 'jig rten gyi khams mi mjed ces bya ba
15b2(khri brgyad): yod de/ de na de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa zhes bya ba da ltar bzhugs te 'tsho zhing gzhes la/ byang chub
15b3(khri brgyad): sems dpa' rnams la chos kyang ston te/ 'di ni de'i mthu yin de dang 'dra'o// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dga' ba'i dpal la/ byang chub sems dpa
15b4(khri brgyad): dga' ba'i byin gyis 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa de la blta ba dang / phyag bgyi ba dang / bsnyen
15b5(khri brgyad): bkur bgyi ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag kyang phal cher gzhon nur gyur pa gzungs dang so so yang dag par rig pa thob pa/
15b6(khri brgyad): ting nge 'dzin dang / snyoms par 'jug pa thams cad la dbang thob pa de dag blta ba'i slang du 'jig rten gyi khams mi mjed du ma mtsha'o// bcom ldan 'ang
15b7(khri brgyad): kyis bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu de'i dus la dbab par shes na khyod song shig/ de na de bzhin gshegs pa dga' ba'i dpal gyis byang chub sems
15b8(khri brgyad): dpa' dga' bas byin la/ pad+ma rin po che sna tshogs kyi rgyu las byung ba gser gyi mdog can mngab ma stong dang ldan pa stong bskur te/ rigs kyi bu khyod
16a1(khri brgyad): kyis de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa la pad+ma 'di dag gtor cing / rigs kyi bu khyod sangs rgyas kyi ning der shes bzhin du spyod cig/
16a2(khri brgyad): phyir zhe na/ 'jig rten gyi khams mi mjed der skyes pa'i byang chub sems dpa' de dag bsnyen par dka' ba'i phyir ro// de na byang chub sems dpa' dga' bas byin
16a3(khri brgyad): gyis/ de bzhin gshegs pa dga' ba'i dpal las rin po che'i rgyu las byung ba pad+ma gser gyi mdog can 'dab ma stong dang ldan pa de dag blangs te/ byang chub sem
16a4(khri brgyad): dpa' khyim pa dang / rab tu byung ba dang / khye'u dang / bu mo bye ba khrag khyig 'bum phrag du mas yongs su bskor cing mdun du bdar te/ lhan cig tu
16a5(khri brgyad): sangs rgyas kyi zhing de nas mi snang bar gyur nas steng gi phyogs na sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ji snyed cig bzhugs te 'tsho zhing gzhes pa de dag thams cad la me
16a6(khri brgyad): tog dang / gdug pa dang / spos dang / me tog 'breng dang / byug pa dang / phye ma dang / gos dang / gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / bdan dag gis/ bsti
16a7(khri brgyad): bstang du byas/ bla mar byas/ ri mor byas/ mchod pa byas nas/ byang chub sems dpa'i rdzu 'phrul chen po dang / byang chub sems dpa'i mthu chen pos 'jig rten
16a8(khri brgyad): gyi khams mi mjed ga la ba der phyin te/ de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa ga la ba der song nas phyin pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag
16b1(khri brgyad): 'tshal te/ phyogs gcig tu 'dug go/ phyogs gcig tu 'dug nas byang chub sems dpa' dga' bas byin gyis/ bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa de la 'di
16b2(khri brgyad): skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dga' ba'i dpal bcom ldan 'das la bskrun gsol te/ gnod pa chung ngam/ nyam nga ba nyung
16b3(khri brgyad): ngam/ bskyod pa yang ngam/ 'tsho ba 'am/ bde bar reg pa la gnas sam/ zhes bskur gsol lo// bcom ldan 'das dga' ba'i dpal gyis pad+ma 'di
16b4(khri brgyad): dag kyang bcom ldan 'das la bskur ro// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pas pad+ma de dag bzhes nas/ steng gi phyogs kyi sangs rgyas
16b5(khri brgyad): bcom ldan 'das gang+gA'i gang gi bye ma snyed de dag ga la ba der logs su gtor to// pad+ma de dag gis kyang 'jig rten gyi khams de dag khyab par gyur te/ pad+ma de dag
16b6(khri brgyad): la sangs rgyas kyi sku dge bzhugs shing sangs rgyas kyi ning de dag na 'di lta ste/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang ldan pa 'di nyid kyi chos bston to// sems
16b7(khri brgyad): gang dag gis chos de thos pa de dag kyang thun meng ba yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu nges par gyur to// de nas byang chub sems dpa' khyim na gnas pa dang
16b8(khri brgyad): rab tu byung ba de dag dang / khye'u dang bu mo de dag gis kyang rang rang gi dge pa'i rtsa ba de dag gis kyang bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pal bsti bstang du byas/
17a1(khri brgyad): mar byas/ ri mor byas/ mchod pa byas te phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// de nas skad cig zang cig yung tsam de la stong gsum
17a2(khri brgyad): stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'di rin po che'i rang bzhin du gnas par gyur te/ me tog sil ma sna tshogs kyis gang ba dang / dar gyi lda ldi mang po bres
17a3(khri brgyad): pa dang / pog bor nas gdug pa dang / dpag bsam gyi shing ston pa rgyan dang / 'bras bu sna tshogs kyis yal ga'i rtse mo g.yur zab dag dang / me tog
17a4(khri brgyad): gi shing ljon pa dag dang / 'bras bu'i shing ljon pa dag dang / spos kyi shing ljon pa dag dang / me tog 'phrong gi shing ljon pa dag dang / phye ma'i shing ljon pa
17a5(khri brgyad): dag gis mdzes par byas par gyur te/ 'di lta ste dper na/ de bzhin gshegs pa kun nas me tog gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing gang na 'jam dpal gzhon nur
17a6(khri brgyad): gyur pa 'dug pa dang / lha'i bu blo gros rab gnas dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gzi brjid che ba gzhan dag kyang gnas pa'i 'jig

17a8(khri brgyad): de'i tshe bcom ldan 'das kyis 'jig rten lha dang bcas pa/ bdud dang bcas pa/ tshangs pa dang bcas pa/ dge sbyong dang bram ze'i skye dgu dang bcas pa

17b2(khri brgyad): bcom ldan 'das kyis tshe dang ldan pa shA ri'i bu la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// shA ri'i bu 'di la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos thams cadarna
17b3(khri brgyad): pa thams cad du mngon par rdzogs par byang chub par 'dod pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la brtson par bya'o// de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / bcom ldan 'ad

17b6(khri brgyad): ldan pa shA ri'i bu la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// shA ri'i bu 'di la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos gnas pa med pa'i tshul du shes rab kyi
17b7(khri brgyad): pha rol tu phyin pa la gnas te/ sbyin par bya ba dang / sbyin pa po dang / len pa po mi dmigs pa'i phyir yongs su gtang ba med pa'i tshul gyis sbyin pa'i pha rol
17b8(khri brgyad): tu yongs su rdzogs par bya'o// ltung ba mi 'byung ba dang / lhag par ltung ba mi 'byung ba'i phyir tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par bya'o//
18a1(khri brgyad): 'khrug pa med pa'i phyir bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par bya'o// lus dang sems kyi brtson 'grus ma btang ba'i phyir brtson 'grus
18a2(khri brgyad): pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par bya'o// ro myang ba med pa'i phyir bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par bya'o// chos thams cad mi dmigs pa'i

18a4(khri brgyad): dmigs pa'i phyir dran pa nye bar bzhag pa bzhi yongs su rdzogs par bya'o// yang dag par spong ba bzhi dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi dang / dbang po lnga dang / stobs
18a5(khri brgyad): dang / byang chub kyi yan lag bdun dang / 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa yongs su rdzogs par bya'o// stong pa nyid kyi ting nge 'dzin dang / mtshan ma med pa'i
18a6(khri brgyad): ting nge 'dzin dang / smon pa ming pa'i ting nge 'dzin bsgom par bya'o// bsam gtan bzhi dang / tshad med pa bzhi dang / gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa bzhi dang
18a7(khri brgyad): rnam par thar pa brgyad dang / mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu dang / 'du shes dgu bsgom par bya'o// dgu gang zhe na 'di lta ste rnam par bam pa'i 'dra
18a8(khri brgyad): shes dang / byed du chad pa'i 'du shes dang / rnam par brnag pa'i 'du shes dang / rnam par dmar ba'i 'du shes dang / rnam par sngos pa'i 'du shes dang / rnam par bos

18b9(khri brgyad): 'dzin dang / mi shes pa kun shes par byed pa'i dbang po dang / kun shes pa'i dbang po dang / kun shes pa dang ldan pa'i dbang dang / zil gyis gnon pa'i skye mched dang /

19a2(khri brgyad): lhag pa'i bsam pa nyi shu dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes dang / zhi gnas dang lhag mthong shes pa dang / rig pa gsum dang / so so yang dag par rig pa ban

20a2(khri brgyad): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bsam gtan dang / ting nge 'dzin

22b8(khri brgyad): par byed pa'i rnam par 'khrug par byed pa'i rlung gi dkyil 'khor de sor mo gcig gi rtse mos gzhil bar 'dod pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o//

23a2(khri brgyad): chen po dang / khor yug dang / khor yug chen po la sogs pa ri gang dag yod pa de dag sla'i nyag ma gcig gis sngams te/ 'jig rten gyi khams grangs med dpag tu
23a3(khri brgyad): med par 'phang ngo // snyam na yang shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o// shA ri'i bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shar phyogs
23a4(khri brgyad): kyi 'jig rten gyi khams gang+gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed dag gi sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das nyan thos kyi dge 'dun dang bcas pa rnams bsod snyoms gcig gis khye
23a5(khri brgyad): par bya bar 'dod pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o// de bzhin du me tog dang / bdug pa dang / spos dang / me tog 'phreng ba dang / byug pa dang /
23a6(khri brgyad): phye ma dang / gos dang / gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan dag gi sngon rnams kyis de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sa
23a7(khri brgyad): sa de dga' bste bsang du bya bar 'dod pa dang / tha mar bya bar 'dod pa dang / ri myor bya bar 'dod pa dang / mchod par bya bar 'dod pas/ shes ra
23a8(khri brgyad): kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o// de bzhin du dag ldan dang / 'phrul dga'i lha rnams kyi nang du skye bar 'gyur/ sbyin pa 'di ltar byin ni bsam/
23b1(khri brgyad): 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par byas pa yi na/ rnam par g.yeng ba dang / kun tu rtogs pa med pa'i phyir bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs
23b2(khri brgyad): su rdzogs par byas pa yin/ chos thams cad rab tu shes/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po lho dang / nu ba dang / byang dang / byang shar dang /
23b3(khri brgyad): shar lho dang / lho nub dang / nub byang / 'og dang / steng gi phyogs re rer yang 'jig rten gyi khams gang+gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed dag gi sangs rgyas bcom
23b4(khri brgyad): ldan 'das nyan thos kyi dge 'dun dang bcas pa rnams bsod snyoms gcig gis khyed par bya bar 'dod pa dang / de bzhin du me tog dang / bdug pa dang /
23b5(khri brgyad): spos dang / me tog dang / byug pa dang / bye sa dang / gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan gyi sprin rnams kyis de bzhin gshegs dgra bcom pa
23b6(khri brgyad): yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas de dag la bste bsang du ba ba 'dod pa dang / bla mar bya bar 'dod pa dang / ri mor bya bar 'dod pa dang / mchod
23b7(khri brgyad): pa bya bar 'dod pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa khri brgyad stong pa/ bram po gnyis pa//
23b8(khri brgyad): shA ri'i bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shir phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams gang+gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed dag na/ sems can ga
24a1(khri brgyad): dag 'khod pa de dag rdul khrims kyi phung po 'god par 'dod pa dang / ting nge 'dzin gyi zang po dang / shes rab kyi zung ba dang /
24a2(khri brgyad): par grol ba'i phung po dang / rnam par grol ba'i ye shes mthong ba'i phung po la 'gong par 'dod pa dang / de bzhin du rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu dang /
24a3(khri brgyad): phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu dang / phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu dang / dgra bcom pa nyid dang / rang byang chub la dgod par 'dod pa dang / phung po lhag ma med bri
24a4(khri brgyad): mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings kyi bar la dgod pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o// shwar thogs la ji sa pa bzhin du lho dang / nub dang /
24a5(khri brgyad): byang dang / byang shar dang / shar lho dang / lho nub dang / nub byang dang / 'og dang / steng gi phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams gang+gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed dag
24a6(khri brgyad): kyang de bzhin du sbyar bar bya'o// shA ri'i bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod cing / sbyin pa
24a7(khri brgyad): byin pa'i tshe/ sbyin pa 'di ltar byin na ni 'bras bu chen por 'gyur/ sbyin pa 'di ltar byin na ni rgyal rigs shong sA la chen pos bu rnams su skye bar 'a
24a8(khri brgyad): de bzhin du bram ze'i rigs shing sA la chen po lta bu rnams dang / khyim bdag gi rigs shing sa la chen po lta bu rnams su skye bar 'gyur/ sbyin pa 'di
24b1(khri brgyad): ltar byin na ni rgyal chen bzhi'i ris kyi lha rnams kyi nang du skye bar 'gyur/ de bzhin du sum cu rtsa gsum pa dang / 'thab bral dang / dga' ldan dang / 'phrul
24b2(khri brgyad): dga'i lha rnams kyi nang du skye bar 'gyur/ sbyin pa 'di ltar byin na ni bsams tan dang po 'thob par 'gyur/ sbyin pa 'di ltar byin na ni gzhan 'phrul dab
24b3(khri brgyad): byed kyi lha rnams kyi nang du skye bar 'gyur/ sbyin pa 'di ltar byin na ni bsam gtan dang po 'gyur/ de bzhin du bsam gtan gnyis pa dang / bsam gtan
24b4(khri brgyad): gsum pa la gnas par 'gyur/ sbyin pa 'di ltar byin na ni bsam gtan bzhi pa thob par 'gyur/ sbyin pa 'di ltar byin na ni nam mkha' mtha' yas skye mched
24b5(khri brgyad): dang / ci yang med skye mched kyi snyoms par 'jug pa thob par 'gyur/ sbyin pa 'di ltar byin na ni 'du shes med min skye mched kyi snyoms par 'jug pa thob pa
24b6(khri brgyad): 'gyur/ sbyin pa 'di ltar byin na ni byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos sum cu rtsa bdun thob par 'gyur/ de bzhin du rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu thob par 'gyur
24b7(khri brgyad): lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu dang / phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu dang / dgra bcom pa nyid thob par 'gyur par shes so// shA ri'i bu gzhan yang byang chub
24b8(khri brgyad): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa/ thabs la mkhas pas sbyin pa 'di ltar byin na ni/ sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa
24b9(khri brgyad): rmoms pa 'jug pa thon por 'gyur/ de bzhin du rnamam pa zhes mtha' yas skye mched dang /
25a1(khri brgyad): yongs su rdzogs par byed/ de bzhin du rdutshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang / bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa dang / brtson
25a2(khri brgyad): 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang / bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par byed do// zhes bya bar
25a3(khri brgyad): bar bya'o// de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / bcom ldan 'das la tshe dang ldan pa shA ri'i bus 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das byang chub
25a4(khri brgyad): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos sbyin pa ci ltar stsal na/ sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par bgyis pa lags/ byang chub sems
25a5(khri brgyad): dpa' sems dpa' chen pos sbyin pa ci ltar stsal na/ tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang / bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa dang / brtson 'grus kyi pha ro/
25a6(khri brgyad): tu phyin pa dang / bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par rabagyis pa lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis
25a7(khri brgyad): bka' stsal pa/ shA ri'i bu sbyin par bya ba dang / gtong ba po dang / len pa po mi dmigs te/ 'khor gsum yongs su dag pas/ sbyin pa'i pha rol/
25a8(khri brgyad): tu phyin pa yongs su dag par byas pa yin na/ ltung ba mi 'byung ba dang / lhag par ltung ba mi 'byung ba'i phyir tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su
25b1(khri brgyad): rdzogs par byas pa yin/ 'khrug pa med pa'i phyir/ bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par byas pa yin/ lus dang sems kyi brtson 'gru
25b2(khri brgyad): ma btang ba'i phyir/ brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par byas pa yin/ rnam par g.yeng ba dang / kun tu rtog pa med pa'i phyir bsam
25b3(khri brgyad): gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par byas pa yin/ chos thams cad rab tu shes pa mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yod
25b4(khri brgyad): su rdzogs par byas pa yin te/ shA ri'i bu byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos sbyin pa de ltar byin na/ pha rol tu phyin pa drug yongs su rdzogs
25b5(khri brgyad): par byas pa yin no// de bzhin du tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa drug po thams cad yongs su rdzogs par byas pa yin no// de bzhin du bzod pa'i pha
25b6(khri brgyad): rol tu phyin pa dang / brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang / bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang / shes rab
25b7(khri brgyad): kyi pha rol tu phyin pa drug yongs su rdzogs par byas pa yin no// shA ri'i bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos sangs rgyas bcom
25b8(khri brgyad): ldan 'das 'das dang ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi yon tan thob par 'dod pas/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslas
26a1(khri brgyad): bar bya'o// shA ri'i bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'jus byas dang / 'dus ma byas kyi chos rnams kyi
26a2(khri brgyad): pha rol tu phyin pa 'gro bar 'dod pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o// shA ri'i bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos 'das
26a3(khri brgyad): ba dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba thams cad kyi de bzhin nyid khong du chud bar 'dod pa dang / de bzhin du chos kyi dbyings skye ba med pa'i mthar phyin par
26a4(khri brgyad): 'dod pas/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o// shA ri'i bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgya

26a7(khri brgyad): dpa' chen po sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi nang gi 'khor du 'gyur bar 'dod pas/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o// shA ri'i bug
26a8(khri brgyad): yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'khor mang po dang ldan par 'dod pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor thob par 'dod pas shes rab kyi pha rol
26b1(khri brgyad): tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o// shA ri'i bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sbyin pa yongs su dag par 'dod pas/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu rtsa
26b2(khri brgyad): ba la bslab par bya'o// shA ri'i bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ser sna'i sems tshar bcang bar 'dod pas shes rab kyi phyin pa la bsku
26b3(khri brgyad): par bya'o// de bzhin du 'chal ba'i tshul khrims kyi sems mi bskyed par 'dod pa dang / gnod sems kyi sems mi bskyed par 'dod pa dang / le lo'i sems
26b4(khri brgyad): dor bar 'dod pa dang / rnam par g.yeng ba'i sems dor bar 'dod pa dang / 'chal pa'i shes rab kyi sems dor bar 'dod pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la
26b5(khri brgyad): bslab par bya'o// shA ri'i bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sems can thams cad sbyin pa las byung ba'i bsod nams bya ba'i dngos
26b6(khri brgyad): po la 'god par 'dod pa dang / tshul khrims las byung ba dang / bsgom pa las byung ba dang / zhal bya ba dang ldan pa dang / rdzas las byung ba'i bsod nams
26b7(khri brgyad): bya ba'i dngos po la dgod par 'dod pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o// shA ri'i bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen
26b8(khri brgyad): mig lnga bskyed par 'dod pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o// lnga gang zhe na 'di lta ste ste/ sha'i mig dang / lha'i mig dang / shes rab
27a1(khri brgyad): kyi mig dang / chos kyi mig dang / sangs rgyas kyi mig dang / de dag bskyed pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o//
27a2(khri brgyad): shA ri'i bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shar phyogs kyi sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das gna'i klung gi byem snyed dag lnga'i mig gi
27a3(khri brgyad): blta par 'dod pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o// de bzhin du khro dang / nub dang / byang dang / byang shangar dang / kar lho dang / smon pa

27a7(khri brgyad): ri'i bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das gang dag phyogs bcu kun gyi 'jig rten gyi khams thams

27b1(khri brgyad): par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas kyi bar du thams cad chud mi za bar bya bar 'dod pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par
27b2(khri brgyad): bya'o// shA ri'i bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'das pa dag gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnams

27b4(khri brgyad): rten na bzhugs ste/ 'tsho zhing gzhes pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnams blta bar 'dod pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu

30a1(khri brgyad): 'bras bu dang / phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu dang / dgra bcom pa nyid dang / rang byang chub dang / bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang
30a2(khri brgyad): chub la dgod par bya'o snyam par shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o// shA ri'i bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de bzhin gshegs
30a3(khri brgyad): pa'i spyod lam la slob par 'dod pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o// shA ri'i bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes ra
30a4(khri brgyad): kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pas 'di ltar brtag par bya ste/ nam zhig na bdag gis glang po che'i lha spangs kyis blta bar bya snyam pa dang ji ltar na bdag sa chen po la
30a5(khri brgyad): rkang pa sor bzhi tsam gyis mi rig par 'gro bar 'gyur snyam pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o// shA ri'i bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sem
30a6(khri brgyad): dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pas 'di ltar brtag par bya ste/ ji ltar na bdag rgyal chen bzhi'i ris kyi lha dang / sum cu rtsa gsum pa dang

30b1(khri brgyad): shin tu mthong dang / mchi dang / mi gdung dang / 'og min gyi lha bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag du ma yongs su bskor cing mdun du bdar te/ byang chub kyi snying por 'gro ba
30b2(khri brgyad): 'gyur snyam na yang shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o// shA ri'i bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa
30b3(khri brgyad): spyod pas 'di ltar yongs su brtag par bya ste/ ji ltar na rgyal chen bzhi'i ris kyi lha nas 'og min gyi ris kyi lha'i bar dag byang chub kyi snying po'i shing drung du bdag gi stan
30b4(khri brgyad): bting bar 'gyur snyam na yang shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o// shA ri'i bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu
30b5(khri brgyad): phyin pa la spyod pas 'di ltar brtag par bya ste/ ji ltar na bdag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas nas 'gro ba dag
30b6(khri brgyad): 'greng ba dang / 'dug pa dang nyal ba'i sa phyogs de rdo rje'i rang bzhin du 'gyur snyam na yang shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o// shA ri'i bu gzhan

30b8(khri brgyad): byung ba'i nyim de nyid la bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur/ mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas nas/
31a1(khri brgyad): nyi ma de nyi ma de nyid la chos kyi 'khor lo bar 'gyur/ 'khor lo bsor nas sems can chang med grangs med pa dag chos la chos

31a4(khri brgyad): brlab par bya'o// shA ri'i bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po zhes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pas 'di ltar brtag par bya ste/
31a5(khri brgyad): ltar na bdag gi nyan thos kyi dge 'dun chad med grangs med par 'gyur/ chos ston pa gcig gis sems can chad med grangs med pa dag stan gcig pa'i byang /
31a6(khri brgyad): chub sems dpar 'gyur zhing bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog par 'gyur/ byang chub sems dpa'i dge 'dun dpag tu med

31a8(khri brgyad): phyin pa la bslab par bya'o// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos ji sa na bdag blan med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs
31b1(khri brgyad): par sangs rgyas pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing de na 'dod chags dang / zhe sdang dang / gti mug gi sa thams cad kyi thams cad du ma grag par 'gyur snyam na yang shes ra
31b2(khri brgyad): kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos ji ltar bdag gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing de na sems can thams cad sbyin pa ni
31b3(khri brgyad): legs pa'o// dul ba ni legs pa'o// legs par sdom pa ni legs pa'o// tshangs par spyod pa ni legs pa'o// chags 'byung po rnams la rnam par

31b6(khri brgyad): bdag gi ming thos pa tsam gyis 'jig rten gyi khams gang+gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed dag na sems can gang dag 'khod pa de dag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa
31b7(khri brgyad): byang chub tu nges par 'gyur snyam na yang des shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la bslab par bya'o// shA ri'i bu gang gi tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' rna
31b8(khri brgyad): po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod cing yon tan 'di dag skyed par byed pa de'i tshe/ stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams na rgyal po chen po bzhi
32a1(khri brgyad): po gang dag 'khod pa 'di snyam du sems te/ sngon gyi de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnam
32a2(khri brgyad): la sngon gyi rgyal po chen po bzhi po dag gis lhung zed dag phul bltar bdag cag gis kyang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'di la lhung zed
32a3(khri brgyad): bzhi dbul bar bya'o// snyam du sems shing yid dga' bar 'gyur ro// sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha rnams dang / 'thab bral dang / dga' ldan dang / 'drul
32a4(khri brgyad): dga' dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha rnams kyang 'di snyam du de lta na lha ma yin gyi ris rnams ni yongs su 'grib par 'gyur zhing lha'i ris rnams ni
32a5(khri brgyad): mngon par 'phel bar 'gyur bar bdag cag gis byang sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'di la rim gro bskyed par bya'o snyam du sems shing yid dga' bar//
32a6(khri brgyad): 'gyur ro// stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams na tshangs pa chen po dag dang / tshangs ris kyi lha nas bzung ste tshangs pa thams cad dang /

32a8(khri brgyad): don du bdag cag gis gsol ba gang ba par bya'o snyam du sems shing yad dga' bar 'gyur ro// shA ri'i bu gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems
32b1(khri brgyad): dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod cing pha rol tu phyin pa drug gis rnam par 'phel ba de'i tshe/ rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo rnams
32b2(khri brgyad): kyang 'di snyam du bdag cag ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'di'i ba dang / ma dang / chung ma dang / bu dang / mdza' bzhes dang / nye du dag sman

333b3(khri brgyad): yin pa de ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ma yin te skye bo med do// tshe dang ldan pa/ ri'i bu rnam grangs des du zhes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i skye ba med pa dang yin pa
333b4(khri brgyad): de ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ma yin no// tshe dang ldan pa sha ri'i bu rang stong pa nyid ni nang stong pa nyid kyis stong do// nang stong pa nyid kyis stong pa nyid gang yin pa
333b5(khri brgyad): de ni nang stong pa nyid ma yin te skye ba med do// dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid kyi bar ni dngos pa med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid kyi bar gyis stong ngo // dngos po med pa'i
